    Enable COOL folder updates during the run

    Split hlterror streams into four separate streams

    select setup with 7 bit L1 TT streaming

    Enables coherent prescales at L2

    Enable Cost Monitoring for online

****** Inner Detector Flags ********************************************************
*
* PreProcessing:
* ==============
*
* run PrepRawDataFormation
* - run new Pixel clustering with splitting using analog information
*   splitting technique:  NeuralNet
* - use X1X masking for SCT readout in reconstruction
* - cut on SCT occupancy for masking noisy modules
* run SpacePointFormation
*
* TrackFinding:
* =============
*
* NewTracking is ON:
* - run SiSPSeededTrackFinder
* - run AmbiguitySolver
* - run TRT_TrackExtension
* - run TrackExtensionProcessor
*   and redo LR and tube hits in fit for TRT !!!
*
* BackTracking is ON:
* - run TRT Segment finding
* - run TRT seeded track finding
*   and load TRT_SeededSpacePointFinder
* - run ambi on TRT seeded tracks
* - create TRT standalone tracks
*
* Cut level for Tracking is set to :  3
*    (1) - 2010 settings
*    (2) - start of 2011 settings
*    (3) - tighter version of (2)
*    (4) - tighten seed d0 cut
*    (5) - seed level 2
*
* slim down the tracks for output on ESD
*
* PostProcessing:
* ===============
*
* run primary vertex finding with IterativeFinding using sorting based on SumPt2Sorting primary vertexing cut setup StartUp
* create TrackParticles
* - and do shared hits search
* - keep extra parameters on track
* run V0 search using conversion finder with secondary vertexing cut setup StartUp
* run conversion finder
* run statistics packages
*
* Other parameters
* =================
*
* solenoid field is ON
*
* Configurable Services loaded:
* =============================
*
* load tracking geometry for Inner Detector
* use Beam Spot Constraint in reconstruction/vertexing
*
* Configurable Tools loaded:
* ==========================
*
* load ROT_Creator for Inner Detector
* load TrackingGeometry
* load Extrapolator:
* - load Runge Kutta propagator
* - load MagFieldTool
* - use material corrections of type 3 in extrapolation and fit
* load MeasurementUpdator
* load track fitter of type  GlobalChi2Fitter
* - refit from ROT
* load PRD_AssociationToolGangedPixels
* load TrackSummaryTool
* - and do holes on track search
*
************************************************************************************
YYYY-MMM-DD hh:mm:ss,nnn  Py:InDetTrigRec_jobOptions.py         INFO Setting up conditions using the new classes
YYYY-MMM-DD hh:mm:ss,nnn  Py:Athena                             INFO including file "InDetTrigRecExample/InDetTrigRecLoadTools.py"
